--
-- Table structure for table `log`
--

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `action` text NOT NULL,
  `user` text NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `imp` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- Table structure for table `oil`

  `oil` text NOT NULL,
  `value` text NOT NULL,
  `type` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
